< Review>
This facility is awesome! It is really really clean and they are really taking the safety of their guests seriously. They check your wellness before you go inside. You are able to make appointments for lap swim which is really cool and they disinfect after. They have arrows on the floor so people are walking in one direction all the staff and guests wear masks. There are even people walking around disinfecting. They moved some equipment outside so your not cramped inside, and you can see how busy they are online before you go. They have a great assortment of workout equipment.I really have been impressed. In a time where businesses are eager to open and are bending the rules on safety guidelines it nice to know that I can go somewhere after work to workout and feel safe. <response>None< /response><pictures>None< /pictures>< review>
What can you say it's the historical YMCA. And in case you didn't know they are a nonprofit that was founded 173 years ago with the goal of doing basically what they are still doing today, making the communities that they serve healthier.  So with all the competition is it a good choice to be your gym? That all depends. If you're single and you like to work out at all hours of the night this probably isn't the place for you because they close at 10 p.m. on the weekdays and 5 on the weekends but if you're a family it's an excellent value at $47 you can bring the whole family they'll even watch your little ones while you work out. They have movie Nights for the kids and they'll even teach your kid to swim and for seniors it's hands down the best place to keep physically fit. The facility at first glance may seem small but they pack a lot in a little space like an arena football field, indoor basketball courts, an indoor swimming pool, free weight room, lots of cardio machines, a Dance Studio, batting cages, a child care center, full locker room with showers. The staff are very professional and provide premium customer service The place has a real exclusive feel to it. So much so that sometimes I have to remind myself I'm at the Y.  The best thing to do if you're not familiar with the place is to go down there and get a 3-day pass, it's free.  You can try it for 3 days and then make up your mind personally it works for me.  I really like it!< /review>

TLDR: overall average 4.25 stars
A solid shabu shabu place. Clean, fresh, good service. You won't be disappointed.

Food: 5/5 stars
Always hot and fresh. Shabu sauce comes with 5 different flavors. 3 different dipping sauces, and various proteins.

Atmosphere: 5/5 stars
Always clean and comfortable. Modern minimalist styling and decorations.

Service:4//5 stars
Fast and efficient.

Expense: 3/5 stars
Medium lunch $20 with tax and tips.  A bit more than average for lunch. Dinner costs about $5 higher.

Return: 4/5 stars</Text>

110717048034465456442<//UserId.>
<name>Johnson Kwong<//name><time>1395871053000<//time>< rating>
3< /rating>
< Text>
Searching for a place to warm ourselves up with food in this cold weather, I came here the other day with my girl for dinner.

To start, I gotta say the prices are pretty expensive for dinner!  It was about $15 for a small rib eye, which contained only 5 pieces!  I do have to say that the meat was pretty fresh though.  In the end, we still got pretty full after eating up all the veggies, udon and rice that came with the order.

There was a choice of three soup bases, I tried the House (chicken broth).  It was nothing out of the ordinary.  The sauces, however, were quite yummy.  The "sa cha" sauce they have were different from the ones I'm accustomed to (in a good way).  It tasted as if it was a mix of the regular "sa cha" sauce found in most hot pot places and the peanut butter sauce.  Together, it created a sauce that is creamy in texture, while still keeping the "sa cha" flavor.  The ponzhu sauce and the peanut butter sauce was the usual fare.

Overall, I think this will probably be a better place to go to for lunch since the prices are more reasonable.< /Text>

< Review>
I adopted a rescue dog last year that had a very bad start in life.  She is a pit bull mix and may have been used as a bait dog for dog fights.  At the same time I took a job where I work at home but occasionally have to travel.  I also was looking for a good daycare where Jade could play and socialize.

I found Canine Retreat.  I made an appointment for Jade to be evaluated by their on site dog trainer.  She spent half a day there with the trainer.  I stayed and watched for about 30 minutes before I left.  Jade is a very shy, very non-trusting little girl.  She was scared and shaking when I turned her over.  The trainer was VERY patient and very gentle with her.  He worked with her for about 20minites before he started ringing other dogs into the area.  Again Jade was scared and nervous.  As soon as I saw she was relaxing a bit I left her for half a day.  When I came back the report was positive and Kade ended up having a good experience.

I drop Jade off about once or twice a day just for fun daycare.  When we are on our way to drop her off, she is crying and singing in the car because she is SO excited to go to daycare.  When she jumps out of the car, she pulls me to get in and is always happy to see the Canine Retreat employee that greets us at the door.  I can log into the WebCam and see what she is doing while I am working.  When I pick her up, I usually get some sort of report on who she played with, what her mood was like etc....

There was one day I dropped Jade off and while I was watching her in the WebCam she got nipped by one of the other dogs while they were playing.  I saw the Canine Retreat employee escort Jade out and about 5-10 minutes later she was brought back in.  When I picked her up that evening, the employee at the front desk looked at Jades end of the day report and immediately told me about the incident and how they handled it.

Even when I board her for work or vacation, they do an excellent job with Jade.  Just like every other dog owner.  Our family would be devastated if anything ever happens to our dog.  I never worry about Jade when I drop her off for daycare or board her for long term stay.  She is always happy to see us when we pick her up and she is always exhausted and goes right to sleep when she gets home.

I love Canine Retreat!!!  I recommend them to any dog owner.  I hired a trainer that was recommended to me from another dog owner at the dog park and even he works with Canine Retreat.  The facility is clean, the employees seem to really care about the dogs and are always kind and welcoming with me.  Even during the Christmas holiday, they put up a tree and were accepting donations for the local pet shelters.

There aren‚Äôt enough words to describe how amazing Canine Retreat is.< /Review>

<rating>5</rating>< Review>
The Bahn Mi Bowl is decent, very filling. The Cilantro overwhelms the meal. The Coconut rice is like a carrier for the ingredients. I request my meal without the beer batter so my review is about the meal without it. I like the way the coconut and cucumbers diffuse the sauce textures. The Crispy tofu is good in a spoonful with the other ingredients and breaks the dulling of the cucumber and Cilantro flavors. The price for the meal is okay. The customer service is on point. The store is open with a decent amount of spacing between seats, wide with high ceilings, and has artwork on the walls.< /Review>

115639227334145751775< /UserId.>
< Time>
1621537764660</Time>
<resp>None</resp>< review>
Great vegan restaurant with some fun plays on popular street comfort foods.  Made a reservation online around noon for 7:30 that night (mid-week).  Overall was a lovely experience.  Definitely coming back.

We ordered the tofu Bahn Mi bowl, the fried mushroom Po Boy, the fried pickles, and added a side of fries to the Po Boy.  A lot of fried food, but it was done perfectly - the last of the fried pickles were still crunchy at the end of the meal.  The mushrooms in the Po Boy were marinated such that my girlfriend (who usually does not like mushroom earthy flavors) thought they were great.  The fries are also worth mentioning: perfect; crunchy on the outside to the last bite, but creamy on the inside.  Looking forward to future meals here.</review>

I stopped at Wild Chive on my drive from LA to San Diego and I highly recommend! I've been vegan for 7 years and have tried a lot vegan resteraunts and this is one of my all time favorites! I do not say this lightly! The produce was incredibly fresh and very clearly picked with love. The food was cooked to perfection! And lets not forget the staff who also deserves a 5 star rating. They were clean, responsive and incredibly thoughtful. I spent some time talking to one of the owners (Wendy - I think) and she has a beautiful story of this woman owned restertaunt. You will not regret the decision to eat here!

P.s. try to BLT - they do NOT skimp on the avacado!< /review>

I had looked online beforehand to try to make a reservation (just in case) and the site wasn't accepting reservations, I wasn't sure if it was due to Covid, if the site was down, or if they were full so I took a chance heading over. Parking is quite limited so I drove down and turned back around and finally lucked out on a spot. I walked in at 2:13pm on Sunday  knowing that they closed at 3pm. When I arrived, there was no one at the front to welcome me and my friend and we were a bit confused about whether to seat ourselves, wait to be seated, go to the bar to order, or otherwise since there was no signage instructing us either way.

When someone finally came out they explained that we should indeed wait so they left and came back about a minute or 2 later. It was then that the person informed us that the kitchen was no longer accepting orders because they closed at 3. This was very disappointing as we had traveled a distance specifically to go here.

While I understand that they were swamped (the establishment was packed and the kitchen was also full of cooks), it is a challenge to know when to patronize an establishment if you can't even show up 45 mins before closing without being turned away. <rate>1<//rate>< Text>
The lack of service is what killed this Buffalo Wild Wings for myself and several work friends.

We ( 8 people in total) arrived at 10 PM to a slightly packed house for a Tuesday night. After getting seating in the Bar Area we sat and conversed as we waited for menus and a server to come by for drink orders.

After 5 minutes of sitting and waiting we grabbed a menu and decided on which foods to order to help when the server came up to get drink orders. We figured help the server and the kitchen along at the same time instead of the time delay waiting for the drinks and ordering.

After a few more minutes, a friend decided to set a timer and see how long it would take for someone to come over and acknowledge us.

After 10 minutes on the timer ( at this point 17 or so minutes had passed) a server came up with menus and told us he would back to take our orders.

5 minutes later ( roughly 23 minutes since we had sat) and no server came by. We got up and left as a server came rushing up to "check on us".

Sorry BWW if this is the service to be expected, then sadly you will not see us here again.

Please be mindful people and call ahead to ensure it is not too busy otherwise what happened to us may happen to you< /Text>

< Text>
I came here with a couple of coworkers late at night and the place is cool and hip. The food was really good, I personally tried the avocado cheese burger and it was wonderful. However, not the best service. Everything was going fine I mean we were stared down a bit at the entrance but nothing peculiar or out of the ordinary.  They took a little while to take drinks but we weren't inpatient. They brought the order out wrong, rootbeers instead of coke, dr pepper instead of sprite. We were all so tired we just ended up swapping drinks. Three of us got burgers and we all got it all mixed up as well, regular onions instead of grilled, onions insted of no onions. Once again we were all so hungry and tired that we ended up just eating it like that, it was still pretty good. We stood up to leave and pay. I understand that she needed to leave but it was a bit embarrassing and she did tell us we could still go sit down after paying but it was kinda humiliating to do so.
